<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a8f78f99-2b4c-40c0-bc5c-08c7860f4ec1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer4916138480395177876"><b>She's ready for the ride of her life . . . </b><br/><br/>Lauren Grahame is looking to reinvent herself. After leaving her cheating husband, Lauren moves to Carnal, Colorado, and gets a job as a waitress in a biker bar called Bubba's. It's a nothing job in a nowhere joint . . . until Tatum Jackson walks in. Lauren has never seen a man with such good looks, muscles, and attitude. But when</span>
  <span id="freeText4916138480395177876" style="display:none"><b>She's ready for the ride of her life . . . </b><br /><br />Lauren Grahame is looking to reinvent herself. After leaving her cheating husband, Lauren moves to Carnal, Colorado, and gets a job as a waitress in a biker bar called Bubba's. It's a nothing job in a nowhere joint . . . until Tatum Jackson walks in. Lauren has never seen a man with such good looks, muscles, and attitude. But when he insults her, Lauren doesn't want anything to do with him. Too bad for Lauren he's also the bar's part owner and bartender.<br /><br />When the rough-around-the-edges Tate meets the high-class Lauren, he thinks she won't fit in at Bubba's. Yet there's more to Lauren than meets the eye, and Tate soon sets his mind on claiming her as his own. Before long, the desire burning between them is heating up the cold mountain air. But when violence strikes the town, Tate must reveal a dark secret to Lauren-one that may put an end to their sweet dreams.</span>

<a href="/questions/480392-is-this-book-a-stand-alone">Is this book a stand alone ?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_480392'><a id="like_count_community_question_480392" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/480392?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">4 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F11227040-sweet-dreams">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/45250556-tarina-deaton"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1463198584i/45250556._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/45250556-tarina-deaton">Tarina Deaton</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Yes and no. Sweet Dreams is book 2 of the Colorado Mountain series, but each book within the series can be read as a stand-alone book as there is no p<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Yes and no. Sweet Dreams is book 2 of the Colorado Mountain series, but each book within the series can be read as a stand-alone book as there is no plot arc between the books. All the books within the ‘series’ are set in the same general, fictional location within Colorado. Characters from the different books may make an appearance, but their story/book is not integral to the plot of the book you are reading. It helps in later books to have read the previous books in the series, but again it’s not enough to confuse you and you won’t get lost. KA does a decent job of explaining any back story you might need to know.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_243030839" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243030839" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243030839?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-contemporary">genre-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243030839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7762557823376045639"><br/><b>Sigh, DNF</b><br/><br/>This was my first -- and last -- book by this author. Her stories may be interesting and heartfelt (according to many of her fans), but her writing is NOT great. I found this book to be nothing more than an unedited rough draft not ready for prime time. More so, she doesn't have a polished writing voice, nor does she have a solid grip of basic writing rules. So if you care about well written stories, be sure to read the free chapters online before you buy. Many readers have been able to</span>
  <span id="freeText7762557823376045639" style="display:none"><br /><b>Sigh, DNF</b><br /><br />This was my first -- and last -- book by this author. Her stories may be interesting and heartfelt (according to many of her fans), but her writing is NOT great. I found this book to be nothing more than an unedited rough draft not ready for prime time. More so, she doesn't have a polished writing voice, nor does she have a solid grip of basic writing rules. So if you care about well written stories, be sure to read the free chapters online before you buy. Many readers have been able to look past the writing issues, so maybe you can too. <br /><br /><b>In full disclosure I only made it 10% (60 pages or so) into it before I couldn't take anymore, so this review is not about the story itself. In truth, she may have told a great story in this book but I will never know. </b><br /><br />So what is wrong with the writing? The major issues I found were:<br /><br /><b>Problem 1:</b> It felt as if HALF the sentences started with the word "I", which to me showed a lack of creative story telling. "I went into...", "I noticed that...", "I couldn't get...". Wow, this got old fast! (Read the first few pages of the <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Sweet-Dreams-ebook/dp/B004XTTSG6/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1323300610&amp;sr=1-1#reader_B004XTTSG6" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams sneak preview</a> and you'll see what I mean. I skimmed the rest of the book and sadly the writing voice issue never stopped.) <br /><br /><b>Problem 2:</b> The loooooong run on sentences are a constant problem, not an occasional one. It is difficult to follow her meandering train of thought through these poorly written sentences. <br /><br />Example: <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"But it hit me just then that since not only did he feel free to shout those things about me when he barely knew me but also he knew I heard it and he didn’t apologize but told me to shake it off and let it go because I should somehow accept he was in a shit mood and just deal with it, that he obviously wasn’t a very nice person and maybe, even though I was a nice person, there were some people who deserved to get back what they got."</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>Problem 3:</b> Poor punctuation, or should I say the lack of it.<br /><br /><b>Problem 4:</b> Parentheses over-kill. She uses A LOT of parentheses to help clarify her meandering thought process. Because of this, the story unfolds in such a choppy manner.<br /><br /><b>Problem 5:</b> Editing. Words like "past" instead of "passed"..etc. Argh. <br /><br /><b>Problem 6:</b> Lack of brevity. A common rule of writing is to omit useless words and repetitive statements. If this book was edited for brevity alone, I bet it would reduce the overall page count by several dozen or more -- at least.<br /><br /><b>Problem 7:</b> The story often meandered making it hard to follow her train of thought. <br /><br />Examples:<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Tonia ignored this totally and I soon noticed she was good at ignoring a lot of things, including me, who she didn’t say so much as “boo” to, and her customers, unless they were good-looking.</i>
</blockquote><br />or<br /><blockquote>
  <i>Her legs had a hint of tan I guessed because she was often out watering her flowers or cleaning the pool or sweeping the walkways or cleaning the cool deck around the pool with a blast from the hose and I noticed she was always in a sundress.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Argh. <br /><br />On a positive note I will say she does a pretty good job of keeping it in an active-voice (show me) instead of a passive-voice (tell me). I mean no offense to those of you who love her books, but she is not an author I'd personally recommend to anyone based on her rough, unedited writing style. <br /><br />This book is a classic example of what Indie authors should not do. There is no excuse to skim over the proofreading and editing steps when publishing a book. Indie authors have a huge uphill battle to prove themselves as worthy as the big name published authors, but as long as such unprofessional manuscripts are being pushed out by Indies that battle will only continue. I honestly couldn't imagine any professional publishing house releasing a manuscript with so many writing errors as this one had. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7762557823376045639" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7986171965372647110"><u>
  <b>TATE IS ON AUDIBLE!!!! Listening to Sweet Dreams.... I love this book <3 </b>
</u><br/>It took me about a week to get through all 25 hours of this audible book, but it was awesome! Just as good as the first time around!!! xoxo<br/><br/><b>5 Dreamy Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/e8bef76d-9e41-468f-8e39-4c67f66c0efe_zpsb1726237.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText7986171965372647110" style="display:none"><u>
  <b>TATE IS ON AUDIBLE!!!! Listening to Sweet Dreams.... I love this book &lt;3 </b>
</u><br>It took me about a week to get through all 25 hours of this audible book, but it was awesome! Just as good as the first time around!!! xoxo<br><br><b>5 Dreamy Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/e8bef76d-9e41-468f-8e39-4c67f66c0efe_zpsb1726237.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381424095i/4842918.jpg" alt=" photo e8bef76d-9e41-468f-8e39-4c67f66c0efe_zpsb1726237.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>I LOVED THIS ONE!</u> Tate Jackson... where have you been all my life? Friends, I am a certified KA addict. I love all her stuff, but this one just went to one of my top KA favorites!<br><br>Lauren has spent the last few months of her life in her car, looking for a place to settle. After suffering the ultimate betrayal, her husband cheating on her and leaving her for her best friend, she lost her something special. She had to get away from her old life. Lauren eventually stumbles into a small Colorado town where she makes friends with the owners of the local motel, and gets a job as a waitress in a biker bar. This is the perfect place for her. Small, unknown, nothing going on. That is the life she wants. Then she sees him, Tate Jackson. <br><br>Tate is part owner of the bar she works at. He is tall, dark, handsome and makes Lauren melt. He is also a bounty hunter, ex cop, and most of the time, an asshole. The two get off to a rough start. Tate comes into the bar mad, says some things he doesn’t mean that Lauren over hears. As time goes on, he apologizes over and over again, eventually, she gets over it. <br><br>The more time Tate spends with Laurie, the more he likes her, the more he wants her. They have a lot of obstacles to jump through. Family issues, evil ex’s (on both ends) and a serial killer on the loose to boot. Despite it all, Lauren has never been happier than when she is with Tate. He’s the only person that can give her Sweet Dreams. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/ccc89197-5502-4666-ab51-89dfb94292c2_zpsdb923ff7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381424095i/4842919.jpg" alt=" photo ccc89197-5502-4666-ab51-89dfb94292c2_zpsdb923ff7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I love it when a book is long, but it doesn’t feel long. This book took a while to read, but I loved every page. I didn’t want it to end. Everything about this book was great, but the best part, hands down was TATE JACKSON &lt;3<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a6542fb8-b9d7-4da5-b95e-54299513a4e6_zps5704c76a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381424095i/4842920.jpg" alt=" photo a6542fb8-b9d7-4da5-b95e-54299513a4e6_zps5704c76a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Which one are you?" I whispered. <br>"What?" he asked. <br>"Are you the good guy, the sweet guy who takes care of me or are you this guy who's kind of a jerk?" <br>His answer was instantaneous. "I'm both those guys, babe. Your job is to get used to it." </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>He could be such a jerk, seriously! But I loved this man! He was sexy, sweet, protective, alpha male and just amazing! His debating with Laurie about the blinds was too funny...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“It isn't that it's too soon, you're on the back of my bike, it ain't too soon. You can buy sheets. You cannot install blinds." <br>"um..." I mumbled. "Can you explain the difference?" <br>"Sheets are chick territory," he said without delay. "You gotta use tools, that's dick territory." <br>"Oh," I whispered. <br>"Don't tread on dick territory," he advised.”</blockquote>
</i><br>I also love his bluntness-<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You just told him-”<br> “I fucked you,” Tate cut me off. “Yeah, I did.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>And one of my favorite things was Jonas, and Tate’s relationship with him.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>“Can you ask your son to stop calling me hot?” “Calls em’ like he sees ‘em babe.”</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Tate and Laurie don’t seem like they would work together, but they have chemistry. They compliment each other. She is under Tate’s skin and he doesn’t want to work her out. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Two kinds of women get under your skin. The ones who do damage, they don't feel good there but once you're fuckin' stupid enough to let them in you got no choice but to take the time it takes to work them out. Then there are the ones who don't do damage, who feel good there, feed the muscle, the bone, the soul, not rip it or break it or burn it. The ones you don't wanna work out.” </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/ee13306f-cca0-4e28-ad3a-5c482fba350d_zps4f813196.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381424095i/4842921.jpg" alt=" photo ee13306f-cca0-4e28-ad3a-5c482fba350d_zps4f813196.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know I’ve spent most of my review gushing about Tate, but I really liked Laurie, too. This was a story of her self discovery, finding that special thing in her life she had been missing. In the end, her life had turned out nothing like she ever would have imagined, but thats okay. It was a million times better than she ever thought was possible. <br><br>Tate and Laurie’s journey was a long one, but it was beautiful. In typical KA fashion, their story not only had romance and steam, but action, suspense, and humor. Once I started this book, I couldn’t put it down. It just gave me the best feeling. Not only were the two main characters amazing, but there was a multitude of secondary characters that made the book with their humor, wit, and love. Another fantastic read that will keep a smile on your face and your heart happy! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/d22fc6d3-73ef-4257-908c-526f2bf417dd_zpsc8aa3b09.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381424095i/4842922.jpg" alt=" photo d22fc6d3-73ef-4257-908c-526f2bf417dd_zpsc8aa3b09.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9903205359118460050">Tate, the "hero" of the book, is a total dick. After he first meets our girl, he calls her a "sorry-ass, old, fat, suburban bitch."<br/>Then, when he realizes that she overheard him say that, he tells her to "shake it off" because he was in a bad mood.<br/>Poor Lauren!<br/><br/><i>

</i><br/><br/>Well, later he decides he likes her and kisses</span>
  <span id="freeText9903205359118460050" style="display:none">Tate, the "hero" of the book, is a total dick. After he first meets our girl, he calls her a "sorry-ass, old, fat, suburban bitch."<br>Then, when he realizes that she overheard him say that, he tells her to "shake it off" because he was in a bad mood.<br>Poor Lauren!<br><br><i>
  <b>If I had a dollar for every time his words in his voice popped into my head and made me flinch the last two days, I could move to the Riviera. They even woke me up in the middle of the night.</b>
</i><br><br>Well, later he decides he likes her and kisses her. He then leaves town for a month without contacting her at all during that time. So, she moves on with her life. She starts working out, gets her hair done, loses weight, and even finds a NICE man that she starts dating. But, then Tate comes back. And, he's pissed (as usual - Tate spends his life angry).<br><br><b>
  <i>"You looked better before, Ace. Now you just look like all the rest."</i>
</b><br><br>Oh, really?? So, when you called her "old, fat, and sorry-assed", you meant that you were attracted to her? Well, it's a wonder that a sweet-talker like you isn't married!! Who wouldn't want a catch like Mr. Charm?<br><br>Well, I guess the answer to that is Lauren. She wants him. The biker who treats her like a doormat half the time and a scapegoat for his anger the other half. I may be a pessimist, but Lauren is a masochist. She let her first husband make her feel bad about herself and now she picks this gem. Have fun letting a guy make you feel like dirt for the rest of your life, girl!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456625211i/18258846._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1628756745" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17130903029169458711"><b>4 Special Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/7662219_zpscbdlvu3j.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462513267ra/19006409.gif' alt=' photo 7662219_zpscbdlvu3j.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Since I've been sick for days now. I don't really feel like doing a huge review. This one will be shorter and to the point. Kinda... I really enjoyed this book. It was angsty, dramatic, and suspenseful without being over the top or driving me crazy. I loved Tate although not as much as Max from book one. I loved Lauren more than Nina from book one. I thought Tate and Lauren had a great relationship full of passion. I will say this book had a lot of similarities with book one. </span>
  <span id="freeText17130903029169458711" style="display:none"><b>4 Special Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/7662219_zpscbdlvu3j.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462513267ra/19006409.gif" alt=" photo 7662219_zpscbdlvu3j.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Since I've been sick for days now. I don't really feel like doing a huge review. This one will be shorter and to the point. Kinda... I really enjoyed this book. It was angsty, dramatic, and suspenseful without being over the top or driving me crazy. I loved Tate although not as much as Max from book one. I loved Lauren more than Nina from book one. I thought Tate and Lauren had a great relationship full of passion. I will say this book had a lot of similarities with book one. Both heroes said Babe as a response to almost every question asked them by the heroine like every 6 or 7 sentences. Both heroines say ummm uhh and sorry at least 10 times a page. And they all talk in half sentences. For example here is what it was like (I made this sentences up not a quote from the book)<br><br>"You doin'?" "Sorry?" " You doing?" "Tate!" "Babe!" "Tate?" "Sick of telling you babe." "Ummm..." "Shut it and kiss me." <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/What-gif_zpskyj6bhxe.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462512666ra/19006343.gif" alt=" photo What-gif_zpskyj6bhxe.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>At times I would have to reread things to try to figure out A) where the hell the first part of all the sentences went? and B)I had to try and decode what each Babe.. Tate and Laurie meant. I am guessing this is going to be one of those author's quirks that KA does a lot. I just hope it doesn't get annoying. Right now I kinda just laugh and shake my head at it but I have a feeling it will get old fast. Now here are a few real quotes from the book showing you what I mean making the one I made up pointless but what the hell...<br><br><i>
  <b>“Um…” I started. He cut me off. “You curl into me.” “Sorry?” I asked. “My back,” he replied. “Um…” I paused then repeated, “Sorry?” “You curl into my goddamned back, Lauren,” he ground out and his arm around my waist gave me a rough squeeze. “I was… uh…”-Lauren and Tate<br><br><br>“Tate!” I snapped. His knee came up, parting my legs. “Bet, way you catch fire, make up sex’ll be hot,” he muttered. “We are not making up and we are not having sex.” His head came up, I saw he was grinning and through his grin he said, “Babe.” “Babe yourself!” I spat.-Lauren and Tate<br><br><br>“Not fun sleepin’ alone,” he muttered into my ear as I pulled against his hold but he was stronger than me and he switched our direction so we were heading to the bed. “Let me go, Tate,” I demanded, my hands shoving at his arm. “Gotta learn to get over it, Ace,” he told me.-Tate and Lauren</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/regret-nothing_zpsrl0ugqbl.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462512667ra/19006344.gif" alt=" photo regret-nothing_zpsrl0ugqbl.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even with the above mentioned KA quirks I still loved this book. I loved all the secondary characters. The bar gang was great. Tate and Lauren made a great couple. I really thought Tate's son Jonas was too cute and there are some really fun moments between Jonas, Lauren and Tate. Tate's Ex was a crazy bitch and I wanted to reach through the kindle and beat the crap outta her. But she was a well developed crazy bitch ex written in a way that made her feel real too. I liked their HEA but not as much as Max and Nina's. I kinda wish they would have had a baby. I know they aren't in their 20s but she was only 42 she could still have a baby. Bottom line I loved this book but I loved the first one better. <br></span>

<div id="review_3548182954" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3548182954" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3548182954?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3548182954" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14989109822565557227"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>HELPPP I’M FALLING DOWN THE KA RABBIT HOLE..........<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600096134ra/30105237.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>..........Actually, please ignore me cause I’m feeling rather comfortable and content here.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600096134ra/30105238.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>My 4th KA book, and each time I finished one, I was astonished by how she managed to make me fall for her story hook line and sinker.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600127639ra/30106710.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>There are a few valid concerns when it comes to KA books—the writing a mess, the push and pull irritating, the length too long, the filler scenes too many, the drama too much, etc. However, to me those a</span>
  <span id="freeText14989109822565557227" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br>HELPPP I’M FALLING DOWN THE KA RABBIT HOLE..........<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600096134ra/30105237.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>..........Actually, please ignore me cause I’m feeling rather comfortable and content here.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600096134ra/30105238.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>My 4th KA book, and each time I finished one, I was astonished by how she managed to make me fall for her story hook line and sinker.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600127639ra/30106710.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>There are a few valid concerns when it comes to KA books—the writing a mess, the push and pull irritating, the length too long, the filler scenes too many, the drama too much, etc. However, to me those are irrelevant cause I thoroughly enjoyed this one.<br><br>↠ <b>Loved Tate.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Two kinds of women get under your skin. The ones who do damage, they don’t feel good there but once you’re fuckin’ stupid enough to let them in you got no choice but to take the time it takes to work them out. Then there are the ones who don’t do damage, who feel good there, feed the muscle, the bone, the soul, not rip it or break it or burn it. The ones you don’t wanna work out.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved Lauren.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“God, if he wasn’t so handsome, strong, sometimes sweet, didn’t have a Harley, that beard, a tendency to play with my hair, didn’t look so good in jeans and wasn’t so danged good in bed, he would seriously not be worth it.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the romance.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m gonna piss you off ‘cause I can be a dick. That’s who I am. And you’re gonna piss me off ‘cause, babe, you got attitude. That’s who you are. And that’s who we’re comin’ out to be together. And I’m all right with that because, with what I had before, even when you’re a bitch, I like it. But when you’re not, it’s a sweetness the like I’ve never tasted.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the small town setting.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“After years of searching, years of longing, years of hoping and then giving up, I’d found special in Carnal and in Tate. Special wasn’t exactly perfect but, even so, it was pretty fucking spectacular and it was finally, finally mine.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the family dynamics.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I spent years tryin’ to shield her from her choices, didn’t work. I’m not gonna let you do it and I’m not gonna teach you that someone’s gonna shield you from shit. You gotta learn too. You make choices, they’re yours and you gotta take responsibility for them.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the humor/domestic vibes.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“We’re buying curtains, babe, that activity hardly requires a cart,” he noted.<br>“We’re in a home store, Tate,” I replied, thinking my answer said all.<br>“And?” he returned, stating plainly my answer did not say all.<br>"A mega home store,” I added.<br>“And?”<br>“And, I came here a few days ago to buy you sheets. I ended up buying you two sets of sheets, six new pillows, a down comforter, a comforter cover and shams. That happens in a home store,” I educated him. “You come in needing a spatula and you go out with a spatula, new kitchen towels, candles, candle holders, cool things to seal open chip bags, a variety of frames, a soap dispenser and a new vacuum cleaner.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the crazy ex drama.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Then you shouldn’t have thrown her away when she was your wife. Now she ain’t. Now she’s somethin’ to me and I don’t let men I don’t like get close to her and I gotta tell you, man, I do not like you.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the cry-me-a-river angst.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You said you were waitin’ for something special and he took away your chance to figure out that you were carryin’ it with you all this time. You are special, Laurie.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved the effing SUSPENSE.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“There’s bad guys out there, Ace. Bad. Do things to you that’ll make you glad you end up dead. You don’t open a goddamned door not knowin’ who’s behind it.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved Jonas.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“An accountant would not make his girlfriend worry he while he was away at work”<br>“Yeah,” Jonas shot back with a smile, “but he also wouldn’t have a milf girlfriend either.”<br>I felt my eyes round as Tate said in a father’s warning tone but still I could tell from his voice he was smiling huge, “Bub.”<br>“Dad, seriously, she’s milf,” Jonas returned.<br>“Think it, boy, don’t say it.” Tate replied.<br>“Right,” Jonas muttered but he was still smiling at me and his smile was unrepentant. Jonas had called me a milf. I knew what that meant and I didn’t know what to do with it. Seriously, Tate from head to toe.”</i>
</blockquote><br>↠ <b>Loved all the side characters.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You give out free bites of your banana bread for a couple of days, you’ll be beating them back with a stick,” I told him. “Hey!” he yelled, his head snapping back to look at me. “Great idea!” Sunny turned to Shambles. “Why didn’t we think of that?” “Because half the time we’re stoned?” Shambles asked back.</i>
</blockquote><br>Nothing I wanted to change, except maybe me wanting to get MORE Jonas content. Tate and Lauren made me wish I had my own sweet dreams. The suspense was pretty intense and brutal. This time, we were dealing with a serial killer. I thought for sure I knew who it was, but I was wrong.<br><br>And the drama!!! KA wrote it so exceptionally (in all the books I’ve read so far) that instead of it turning you off, you actually CRAVED it. Seriously, it wasn’t annoying at all but hilarious and entertaining while also still made me a little bit sympathetic towards the antagonists.<br><br>I think this might be my favorite KA book. It had a combination of everything without making it feel contrived and made me feel all the feels. I just loved it. Do yourself a favor, and get the AUDIOBOOK if you can cause . . . *exclaims in true KA fashion* . . . IT’S THE SH*T!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_616209335" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/616209335" />
    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/616209335?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781538744352" href="/book/show/33161428-sweet-dreams">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=price-was-right-2-99-or-less">price-was-right-2-99-or-less</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616209335" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4606727522725072438">Okay, <i>THIS</i> is my very last <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a>. I know I said that the last time I tried her, but this time it's for realsies. <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> is super popular with all my friends, and I've met her in person (she is very sweet), but I'm just accepting the fact that I <i>hate</i> her books. <br/><br/>I bought this one to try in paperback (I've tried her books in every format, attempting to see if I could like them), but I ended up rage highlighting passages instead of enjoying the story. <b>I think Kristen Ashley and I fu</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4606727522725072438" style="display:none">Okay, <i>THIS</i> is my very last <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a>. I know I said that the last time I tried her, but this time it's for realsies. <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> is super popular with all my friends, and I've met her in person (she is very sweet), but I'm just accepting the fact that I <i>hate</i> her books. <br /><br />I bought this one to try in paperback (I've tried her books in every format, attempting to see if I could like them), but I ended up rage highlighting passages instead of enjoying the story. <b>I think Kristen Ashley and I fundamentally have different tastes on most topics.</b><br /><br /><b>Now I'm going to get REAL critical up in here, so if you are tempted to fight on KA's behalf, please don't read on. </b><br /><br />I thought, buying the paperback, that the editing would be improved. Spoiler alert: it wasn't. I'm talking <b>run on sentences, grammatical errors, lack of punctuation</b>... it was hard to read at times. <br /><br />My next issue is sort of bitchy, but <b>I couldn't <i>stand</i> the endless wardrobe descriptions.</b> I mean, every <i>single</i> item of clothes the MC wore, we got a detailed description. I'm talking head to toe (I'm surprised her bra wasn't described with each outfit). And (and here is the real catty part), but the outfits were all <i>hideous</i> 90s-style strange clothes. I actually went to check the date of publication because the wardrobe felt 25 years out of date (the book was written in 2011). <br /><br />Finally, <b>I think Kristen Ashley and I just don't see eye-to-eye on what's healthy and attractive male-female interaction.</b> I found Tate to be impossibly rude, pushy, and smug. I wanted to punch him in the face. My type is more nerdy, intellectual guys (preferably with facial hair and glasses), and Tate was the muscle-obnoxious guy of my nightmares. I don't care that KA makes Tate "right" most of the time and Lauren bashfully wrong- I couldn't stand him. <br /><br />I DNF-ed the paperback at ~350 pages (too long!!), and I won't look back. I'm out. <br /><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time" rel="nofollow noopener">goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.instagram.com/reading_all_night_long/" rel="nofollow noopener">instagram</a>|<a href="https://twitter.com/DentistHeatherK" rel="nofollow noopener">twitter</a>|<a href="http://www.myfictionnook.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4606727522725072438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer241877783" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14082359290847301462"><b>EDITED December 15, 2011 and January 1, 2012</b><br/>On the one hand, I agree that the story needed better editing. On the other hand, Tate would say "Who gives a flying f*ck?" I wholeheartedly agree, Tate! I didn't mind at all. I LOVE this story and I could easily forget those minor issues. <br/>************************************************************************<br/><b>Tate with beard:</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/FUN/MEN-AND-MEN-WOMEN/?action=view&current=Bildschirmfoto2012-09-14um194424.png' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b>Tate without beard:</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/FUN/MEN-AND-MEN-WOMEN/?action=view&current=AnsonMount2011WiredStoreOpeningNightnW1hEj29KX1l.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b>"How blessed are some people, whose lives have no fears, no dreads; to whom sleep is a blessing that </b></span>
  <span id="freeText14082359290847301462" style="display:none"><b>EDITED December 15, 2011 and January 1, 2012</b><br>On the one hand, I agree that the story needed better editing. On the other hand, Tate would say "Who gives a flying f*ck?" I wholeheartedly agree, Tate! I didn't mind at all. I LOVE this story and I could easily forget those minor issues. <br>************************************************************************<br><b>Tate with beard:</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/FUN/MEN-AND-MEN-WOMEN/?action=view&amp;current=Bildschirmfoto2012-09-14um194424.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379778944i/385684._SY540_.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Tate without beard:</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/FUN/MEN-AND-MEN-WOMEN/?action=view&amp;current=AnsonMount2011WiredStoreOpeningNightnW1hEj29KX1l.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364134i/715701._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"How blessed are some people, whose lives have no fears, no dreads; to whom sleep is a blessing that comes nightly, and brings nothing but sweet dreams."<br>- by Bram Stoker -<br><br>"What lies behind us, and what lies before us are tiny matters compared to what lies within us."<br>- by Ralph Waldo Emerson -</b><br><br><b>H.U.G.E. 5 stars!</b><br><br><i>EXCELLENT. TERRIFIC. FABULOUS. GREAT. WONDERFUL. BEAUTIFUL. REALISTIC. EMOTIONAL.</i> Wow, did I miss anything? I absolutely LOVED, LOVED Sweet Dreams! Jeez, what's not to love about this story? It was an enlightening reading experience. Irrevocably. Sweet Dreams is my favorite book to date. Ever. Tate, you uber-hot, badass (badass with a capital B), sexilicious specimen of a man…awwww, you are definitely the epitome of Mr. Hotness in high perfection! You are such a bossy, demanding, and annoying jerk at times, yet you are so caring, protective, sweet, and tender…my stomach just flipped. Again. YUM! *dreamy sigh* Speaking about attitude…Seriously, Tate, you're talking about Laurie having attitude? Yeah, man, what about you, huh??? You've got a serious case of attitude. Tsk-tsk…<br><br>The hero is the personification of a badass biker bounty hunter, and therefore he 'likes' to use the f-word regularly. Please, don't let it put you off. Basically, I don't like that either, however in this case it suited the hero, and I wouldn't have it any other way. Tate stayed true to his character and everything he said and did helped to show the reader what a wonderful man he is. I'd like to alert you. Don't jump to conclusions too fast in the beginning of the story. It's what Lauren did…Tate said something nasty, but I forgave him, since he had some serious s*it going down in his life. As the story unfolds you'll get to know him better and even Lauren will have to admit that she made a 'mistake'. Don't judge too fast. Just sayin'…<br><br>Admittedly, I am always so focused on the hero, yet Sweet Dreams features a superb heroine. Wow, Lauren kicks ass! Even when she is kind of 'lost' in the beginning of the plot, she can hold her own. She is sassy and a real smart-mouth. I adored this woman! And Tate will help her find herself again - she has to get rid of her being 'lost'.<br><br>Sweet Dreams lives and breathes dialogs - lots and lots of wonderful and hilarious dialogs! This story put a smile on my face, and there were many laughing-out-loud moments too. I was glued to the pages and I truly regretted the fact that it had to end eventually. Boy, I can't get enough of these two! On top of that, the author did a very fine job in developing many secondary characters as well. They're complex, yet so endearing. BTW, the story is told in first person POV and my advice to those who don't like that…read it nevertheless! It was truly perfect. And after awhile I didn't even notice it anymore. I was so focused what would happen next that I didn't mind at all.<br><br>I loved the author's detailed, very engaging, and colorful writing. It never felt contrived; it was real and emotional. She writes like she'd paint a picture - a very vivid and colorful picture, that is. There's certainly nothing black and white about her story. Do you remember how it feels to look at a wonderful picture? You think you've seen everything and then suddenly in a corner you'll discover something new. With that said, reading Sweet Dreams felt like discovering a good picture, a very interesting and enticing picture. Frankly, it was a very long read (about twice as long as a usual novel), and Ms. Ashley was always able to keep me on my toes. She did it with such ease and lightness…wow, I was in awe! Honestly, there was never a dull moment throughout the storyline. The pace was very good, it never dragged but there was no need to rush things either.<br><br>The character and plot development were exemplary; the sex/love scenes were well written. They are not very long but they showed desire, passion, sensuality, hotness, and love! Sheesh, they had such terrific chemistry and they really needed each other and they showed it. And Tate got hands and a mouth…mmmm…I was salivating. Actually, there was a lot of touching and it felt so real - I was right there and every word and every touch just leaped off the page. And their necking was so sweet! *dreamy sigh - again* Additionally, it was rewarding to read about their everyday business - for instance when they went shopping. I felt like I was there and I was silently laughing when Tate had to push the cart (actually, he was half-lying on the cart) and Mr. Hotness was not at all amused. Ehm, Tate, do you remember…chick territory! LOL Furthermore, it was so endearing to read about their family dynamics (Lauren's family is wonderful). Sweet Dreams just grabbed me and I couldn't let go anymore. The characters will stay close to me. <b>Tate, I promise you a very special place in my heart and I love you to pieces! Always.</b><br><br><br>Ms. Ashley came up with some funny names:<br>La-La Land (coffee shop), Sunray Goddess (Sunny, a hippie woman), Shambala (Shambles, a hippie guy), Bubba (a guy and the name of the biker bar), Chantelle - that's a town (BTW, Chantelle is also a French brand for lingerie), Gnaw Bone (another town), Wood (another guy, hmmm…sorry, but my mind is wandering elsewhere).<br><br><i>Brief synopsis:</i><br>Lauren Grahame is sitting in her parked car outside Bubba's biker bar in Carnal, Colorado. She looks at the window of the bar. In it there's a sign that says "Help Wanted". In the little white space at the bottom of the sign is written, "Waitress". Lauren enters the bar and applies for the waitress position. As long as Lauren can remember she thought something special was going to happen to her. She felt that it had to be something special, something huge…But it didn't. She waited and it didn't happen. Even when she tried to make it happen, it still didn't happen. Eventually Lauren gives up, since there isn't anything special out there to happen. Boy, was she ever wrong!<br><br>Lauren had a husband, a home, a job, and friends. Lauren's husband cheated on her for five years (with her best friend); he divorced her. They had to sell their house and after ten years of being with someone, she was alone. She quits her job and drives around and arrives in Carnal. Lauren gets the job. And she finds something…special and huge in Carnal. Tate Jackson enters her life. He is 44 years old and one of the bar owners. Tate works as a bartender and bounty hunter. Their first 'official' meeting sucks, because she overhears Tate saying:<br><br><i>Behind closed doors…<br>"Jesus, Krys, maybe you wanna talk to me before you hire some sorry-ass, old, fat, suburban bitch to drag around our goddamned bar?"</i><br><br>Admittedly, I was so not pleased to hear that, but as I mentioned before something bad happened to Tate, and he will apologize for being such a jerk. Just cut him some slack.<br><br>It seems that Lauren went from a pansy-assed dickhead (her ex) to a badass bounty hunter in the space of a year… :D<br><br>***********************************<br><br><b>Aw, there is so much to LOVE about this story, and there are so many, many memorable dialogs between Tate and Lauren. I put my memorable "quotes"/lines in a spoiler. You may read them though, since I didn't include any spoilers. Enjoy!</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Tate said:<br>&lt;…&gt;"You want sweet dreams, lose the attitude and you might find I'll give you reason to have them." &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Like I said, when I get pissed I say a lotta shit I don't mean and what I said about you I didn't mean," he repeated, beginning to look as impatient as he sounded.<br>"And like I said, you're old enough to learn you shouldn't do that," I repeated too, probably also looking impatient.<br>"That isn't me," he replied.<br>"Well, then, this obviously is eating you and that's your consequence because I have feelings and you walked all over them and you can't order me to shake it off so you can feel better. It's there, burned in my brain and I can't just forget it because you tell me to. So you have to live with that. You can't and want me gone, say it now because I'm beginning to like Betty and I met Shambles and Sunny and I'm having dinner with them tomorrow night and I'd rather not make ties when I'm going to need to hit the road because my boss is going to get rid of me."<br>"Shambles and Sunny?" he asked.<br>"Shambles and Sunny," I answered but didn't share more. "Now, can we just move on and do our best to work together and all other times avoid each other or do you want me to go?"<br>He moved forward an inch and I again fought the urge to retreat.<br>"Forgiveness is divine," he said softly and I'd never heard him talk soft. He had a very nice voice but when it went soft, it was beautiful.<br>This also sucked. (BTW, in the beginning a lot of things sucked! :D) I mean Lauren uses this word 'sucks'.<br>"I'm not divine," I returned. "I'm also not Ace and I'm not Babe. I'm Lauren. You don't like my name, don't call me anything at all. Now can I clean the danged table?"<br>I had my head tipped back to look him in the eye but I could tell he was expending effort to hold his whole body still.<br>Then he said in that soft voice, "I'm sorry, Ace."<br>"Me too," I replied instantly being clear I didn't accept his apology... &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Ace!" Tate shouted, both Wendy and I jumped and twisted our necks to look his way. "You cashed out or what?" Tate asked still in a shout.<br>"I'm cashed out," I shouted back.<br>"You wanna socialize for the next hour or are we gonna go?" He was still shouting and I was acutely aware, due to the fact that the noise level declined significantly, that the entire bar was listening.<br>"Keep your pants on!" I yelled.<br>The noise level disappeared.<br>"Babe, get your ass over here," Tate ordered.<br>"Patience, Captain, I'm talking to Wendy," I shot back.<br>"Ass. Over. Here!" Tate commanded.<br>I looked at Wendy and snapped loudly, "He's so darned bossy!"<br>Two men and a woman sitting at the bar close to us burst out laughing.<br>"You better get your ass over there," Wendy advised, I rolled my eyes and stomped across the bar. &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;His smile got even bigger. "Yeah, Ace, a day of you cryin' in my arms, sleepin' in my arms, kissin' you, feelin' your body, smellin' your hair, your perfume, only so much a man can take. I ran for an hour, hard, didn't even fuckin' warm up, it didn't touch it. Come back, deal with that fuckwad, (that's her ex) and you're standin' there, all legs and hair, wearin' my shirt. Seriously. Only so much a man can take." &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Two of us in this room, Ace, two keycards," he said and my eyes went to him. When they did, he jerked his hand, finger extended to the door. "Know what this is?"<br>"A door?" I asked stupidly.<br>"A peephole," he bit back then moved his hand to flick the security latch closed. "Know what that is?"<br>"Captain -"<br>He advanced and the aggressive way he did it made me retreat. It was dawning on me he was pissed and he wasn't pissed at Brad (that's her ex). He was pissed at me.<br>I stopped when my legs hit the chair to the desk. He stopped when he was in my space. I tilted my head way back to look at him.<br>"You got great hair, babe."<br>"Tate -"<br>"Thick."<br>"Tate -"<br>"Soft."<br>"Tate," I whispered.<br>"Shame it gets hacked off with a knife after some guy rapes you with that knife!" He finished on a roar.<br>My body jolted.<br>"Tate!"<br>"There's bad guys out there, Ace. Bad. Do things to you that'll make you glad you end up dead. You don't open a goddamned door not knowin' who's behind it."<br>"I thought it was you."<br>"Well it wasn't."<br>"Tate -" &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Which one are you?" I whispered.<br>"What?" he asked.<br>"Are you the good guy, the sweet guy who takes care of me or are you this guy who's kind of a jerk?"<br>His answer was instantaneous. "I'm both those guys, babe. Your job is to get used to it."<br>There it was, another order. Not even an ultimatum. Just, "get used to it".&lt;…&gt;<br><br>I loved this bathroom scene - this is only a little part of it:<br>&lt;…&gt;"Jesus, Laurie, baby, look at you."<br>My eyes followed his, mainly because I wanted him to keep at me and I'd do just about anything he told me to do to get it.<br>But what I saw made my heart skip and my legs fail.<br>Tate, dark, tall, behind me, his hands on me; me, blonde, my face flushed, my eyes hooded, tucked tight against him. A perfect fit, made to be there. A perfect match, made to be together.<br>Made to be there.<br>Made to be together.<br>We looked great.<br>We looked hot.<br>We looked beautiful.<br>My eyes went to his in the mirror.<br>And she said…&lt;…&gt; too bad you'll have to read it - awwww, I know, I know I am such a tease! LOL <br><br>Tate to Lauren's ex:<br>&lt;…&gt;"Then you shouldn't have thrown her away when she was your wife. Now she ain't. Now she's somethin' to me and I don't let men I don't like get close to her and I gotta tell you man, I do not like you." <br>&lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"It isn't that it's too soon, you're on the back of my bike, it ain't too soon. You can buy sheets. You cannot install blinds."<br>"um..." I mumbled. "Can you explain the difference?"<br>"Sheets are chick territory," he said without delay. "You gotta use tools, that's dick territory."<br>"Oh," I whispered.<br>"Don't tread on dick territory," he advised.<br>"So, um... is a paintbrush a tool?" I asked cautiously.<br>"If you're paintin' the side of the house, yeah. If you're painting mud colored paint in a room, no."<br>"It's terracotta," I said softly.<br>"Whatever," he muttered, his mouth twitching.<br>"Or, the paint chip called it Mexican horizon. The blue is dawn sky."<br>"Definitely chick territory," Tate replied, losing the fight with his grin.<br>"What about...pictures for the walls?" I asked.<br>"Chick," he answered instantly.<br>"Um...could I ask that, instead of you getting angry and being a jerk, maybe you give me a head's up when I'm doing something stupid?" &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"I wanted to play ball," he stated in a way that my body got very still and my eyes, already locked to his, became glued there. "It wasn't the money. It wasn't the fame. It was the game. The goddamned game. I didn't feel like I was breathin' right if I wasn't playin' or practicin'. Felt like life was still, someone hit pause, then I'd put on my pads and jersey and walk on the field and then everything would come alive. Dad and I were Eagles fans since I could remember. Puttin' that fuckin' jersey on, Christ, Laurie...Christ." &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Three weeks, after fuckin' you, knowin' what you taste like, what you feel like, the sounds you make when you come, three weeks I'm on the road and all I got is a couple minutes of your voice on the phone every night. Fuckin' you, that's all I can think about, like a teenager, at night in the dark, it's the only thing in my goddamned head. So I jack off, hopin' to cut through it, but nothin' compares to you. Then I know you can't sleep so I can't fuckin' sleep wonderin' if you're sleepin'. That shit's whacked and I come home, fuckin' beside myself it's over."<br>"So we find out about each other and who we are together. I'm gonna piss you off 'cause I can be a dick. That's who I am. And you're gonna piss me off 'cause, babe, you got attitude. That's who you are. And that's who we're comin' out to be together. And I'm all right with that because, with what I had before, even when you're a bitch, I like it. But when you're not, it's a sweetness the like I've never tasted."<br>"You said you were waitin' for something special and he took away your chance to figure out that you were carryin' it with you all this time. You are special, Laurie." &lt;…&gt;<br><br>&lt;…&gt;"Two kinds of women get under your skin. The ones who do damage, they don't feel good there but once you're fuckin' stupid enough to let them in you got no choice but to take the time it takes to work them out. Then there are the ones who don't do damage, who feel good there, feed the muscle, the bone, the soul, not rip it or break it or burn it. The ones you don't wanna work out." &lt;…&gt;<br><br>Wow, this was so hilarious:<br>&lt;…&gt;Brad (Lauren's ex) ignored Hayley (she's Brad's ex girlfriend) and looked at me, he did a top to toe and back again then his gaze moved to Tate.<br>"I'm here to tell you I'm suing you," he announced.<br>Jim-Billy, Nadine, Steg, Wing and my eyes moved to Tate.<br>Tate stared at Brad then he said, "Come again?"<br>"I'm suing you," Brad repeated.<br>"For what?" Tate asked.<br>"Alienation of affection," Brad answered.<br>Without hesitation, Tate threw his head back and burst out laughing.<br>Then he looked at me and remarked, "You're right, babe, this is fun."<br>Ignoring Tate's comment, Brad declared, "You stole my wife."<br>Tate looked back at Brad. "Yeah, bud, I did."<br>Brad pointed at Tate and his voice was raised when he proclaimed, "See? You admit it." He threw his arm out. "I have witnesses."<br>"Not that any judge'll hear your case, seein' as Lauren divorced your ass before I alienated her affection, but you manage it, I'll pay the fine. In the meantime, I'll keep alienating her affection. You should know, and feel free to share it with your lawyers," Tate continued magnanimously, "schedule's comin' out mornin' and night. Usually, in the mornin', she sucks me off or I make her come in the shower. Night, man…shit, that's even better. Definitely worth the fine."<br>Sorry, it's just too long; I have to cut it off. But it continues…like that:<br>"This is the good life?" (Brad)<br>"Part of it," Tate replied instantly, taking his fists from the bar, leaning into his forearms and asking softly, in a tone meant both to challenge and provoke, "She ever ignite, lose so much control she'd attack you? Climb on top and fuck you so hard she can't breathe?"<br>I watched Brad suffer that blow because I hadn't, not even close. We'd had good sex but not that good and Brad was extremely proud of his sexual prowess. He was convinced he was the best. And he knew, with Tate's words, he was wrong.<br>"Jesus, you're disgusting," Brad muttered, calling up revulsion to save face.<br>"She does that to me," Tate continued.<br>"Fuck off," Brad snapped.<br>"All the fuckin' time," Tate pushed.<br>"Fuck off," Brad repeated.<br>"It's fuckin' magnificent," Tate declared.<br>"Thanks, honey," I whispered and grinned at him when his eyes came to me.<br>I was actually expressing gratitude, although embarrassed by his conversation, but I was also kind of joking to get in Brad's face.<br>Tate wasn't. His expression was serious when he said, "You are, Ace. Fuckin' magnificent."&lt;…&gt; <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>I'm going to plow right through Ms. Ashley's backlist. Today I had to download six books at once, and I assume that I'll be busy for the next few days/weeks. Sweet Dreams is such an engaging, outstanding, and wonderful story with great characters. It is not only a love story. It's about life, about people, and about finding yourself and what you want out of life. <b>I'd like to give you exactly one advice: READ IT!!!</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_258093485" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/258093485" />
    <a title="Shawna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna"><img alt="Shawna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574172018p2/1802746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/258093485?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of contemporary romance &amp; hot alpha heroes</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shawna by: </span>
      My fellow alpha lovin’ sista Yvonne...and practically everyone else!
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-silent-quiet-type-reticent">hero-silent-quiet-type-reticent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-asshat-award-hall-of-shame">hero-asshat-award-hall-of-shame</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=romance-doesnt-end-at-40">romance-doesnt-end-at-40</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-i-disliked-much-of-the-book">hero-i-disliked-much-of-the-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=format-ebook">format-ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=small-town-lovin-small-town-setting">small-town-lovin-small-town-setting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hh-sweet-nice-paired-vs-gruff-cynic">hh-sweet-nice-paired-vs-gruff-cynic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=editing-nightmare">editing-nightmare</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-stud-mantel-hall-of-fame">hero-stud-mantel-hall-of-fame</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer258093485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6052949491653634116">5+ stars – Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br/><br/>There are a lot of reviews for this already, so here are some of my random thoughts.<br/><br/><u>The Bad and The Ugly</u>:<br/> <br/>•Yes, it’s an editing nightmare that at times made me want to whip out my red pen and go crazy with correcting remarks. <br/>•There is way too much (and occurring too often) inane detail, especially about the heroine’s wardrobe, outfits, hair, makeup, getting ready, routine, etc. I understand that her self-esteem and makeover were a significant com</span>
  <span id="freeText6052949491653634116" style="display:none">5+ stars – Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br><br>There are a lot of reviews for this already, so here are some of my random thoughts.<br><br><u>The Bad and The Ugly</u>:<br> <br>•Yes, it’s an editing nightmare that at times made me want to whip out my red pen and go crazy with correcting remarks. <br>•There is way too much (and occurring too often) inane detail, especially about the heroine’s wardrobe, outfits, hair, makeup, getting ready, routine, etc. I understand that her self-esteem and makeover were a significant component to the story, but I still think an easy 50+ pages of random “stuff” could have been trimmed. <br>•It was annoying to me how the heroine constantly answered the hero with “Sorry?”, and also how she repeated Tate’s name over and over again like Kate Winslet’s Rose continually said “Jack”, “Jack”, “Jack”, “Jack” all throughout <i>Titanic</i>. <br><br><b>BUT</b>, despite those annoyances, here’s why I still rated it 5 stars.<br><br><u>The Good</u>:<br><br>•The story has a frenetic hodgepodge of themes: chick lit self-discovery, steamy contemporary romance, small town drama, family angst, crazy exes, serial killer suspense...you name it. But amazingly enough, it works. I was sucked in and thoroughly entertained.<br>•The hero is an ex-football star, ex-cop, bounty hunting, bar-owning, tattooed badass, uber alpha biker. He’s growly, sometimes mean, often pissed off, possessive, and fond of saying (or perhaps I should say grunting) “Babe” and “Ace” to communicate a wealth of things, rather than expressing or explaining himself. There were times I wanted Lauren to smack him and send his ass packing to the curb. But <i>DAYUM</i>! Tate is <i>f’n HOT</i>! <br>•The heroine is insecure, funny, flawed, sweet, sometimes cranky and bitchy, caring, and most of all, genuine and endearing. Laurie is easy to identify with because she’s so real. I could see myself laughing over manis and martinis with her. <br>•Cute scenes with Buster the cat, aka, Princess Fancy Pants. <br>•Tender, heartbreaking moments with Tate’s son, Jonas. *sigh*<br>•An unforgettable, quirky cast of secondary characters. <br>•Great dialogue, snappy banter, humor, and emotion. It made me laugh out loud at times and tear up in others. <br>•And oh yeah, the steamy romance between Tate and Laurie is truly addictive.<br><br>So it’s not perfect, but I still <i>loved</i> it and will definitely read more by this author!<br><br>I had a hard time casting my perfect Tate, mainly because he’s so impossibly gruff, badass, and smokin’ hot. But I think Hugh Jackman could portray him fairly convincingly, especially if he acted all Wolverine broody, growly, alpha badass and got some sexy tats. He particularly looks the part in these pictures. YUMMY! <br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=hugh-jackman-per-vanity-fair-47200asp34853img1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366743i/719076.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=5b902ac13b20091jpg.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366743i/719077.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Addendum after further Internet exploration for the perfect Tate:</i><br><br>This is Tate in all his beautiful, badass, bounty hunter glory. *sigh*<br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=Joe-Manganiello.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379765915i/241401.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/237985351?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

      Everyone!

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characters">fabulous-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-hero">favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=scrumptious-hero">scrumptious-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=all-time-favorite">all-time-favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=great-ending">great-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characterizations">fabulous-characterizations</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer237985351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14896926242177833031"><b>HUGE 5+ stars</b><br/><br/>To say I love <i>Sweet Dreams</i> is an understatement! This is one of those books that not only captures your heart and imagination, but brands itself on you personally and will always, in someway, be a part of you. <br/><br/><i>Sweet Dreams</i> encompasses everything I love in a romance novel. It's chock-full of richly developed and unique characters, excellent and witty dialogue, steamy but tasteful eroticism, and captivating and exceptional storytelling. <br/><br/>This book is a self published work and there is </span>
  <span id="freeText14896926242177833031" style="display:none"><b>HUGE 5+ stars</b><br /><br />To say I love <i>Sweet Dreams</i> is an understatement! This is one of those books that not only captures your heart and imagination, but brands itself on you personally and will always, in someway, be a part of you. <br /><br /><i>Sweet Dreams</i> encompasses everything I love in a romance novel. It's chock-full of richly developed and unique characters, excellent and witty dialogue, steamy but tasteful eroticism, and captivating and exceptional storytelling. <br /><br />This book is a self published work and there is no arguing it needs a major editing overhaul. The prose is verbose, ambiguous, and even jarring at times. It's full of typos, run on sentences, punctuation and spelling errors. It's a big ol' mess. BUT, I'm afraid a good editor would inadvertently change what I love so much about this book—It's rawness and personal tone, as well as the author's intimate connection with the reader. <br /><br />The cast of motley characters in this book are multi-dimensional, fascinating, and simply spectacular. The two main protagonist, Tate (Oh My!) and Lauren, complement each other perfectly and their steamy chemistry radiates off the pages. I found myself eagerly looking forward to their passionate, heart-warming, erotic, and witty interactions. They definitely earned a spot as one of my all time favorite couples. The secondary characters were just as enchanting as the protagonists and made this story even better. <br /><br />I honestly can't rave about this book enough. These characters will alway have a special place in my heart. I can't think of a better gift an author can give to her reader. I most definitely recommend this book.  <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>
