        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer262719270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10937500894649484603"><br/><i>Sweet Dreams</i> is the second book in the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series and another fantastic read. As is the case with the first book, <i>The Gamble,</i> there are already dozens of awesome reviews, so I’ll keep mine short, and still try to list my favorite things about this story.<blockquote>1.	Tate is an asshat. He’s got a foul mouth, short fuse, and he’s over the top alpha. He’s honorable, hard working and completely devoted to his friends, family, and those who don’t piss him off. He is, in a word, perfect.<br/>	<br/>2.	The wr</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10937500894649484603" style="display:none"><br /><i>Sweet Dreams</i> is the second book in the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series and another fantastic read. As is the case with the first book, <i>The Gamble,</i> there are already dozens of awesome reviews, so I’ll keep mine short, and still try to list my favorite things about this story.<blockquote>1.	Tate is an asshat. He’s got a foul mouth, short fuse, and he’s over the top alpha. He’s honorable, hard working and completely devoted to his friends, family, and those who don’t piss him off. He is, in a word, perfect.<br />	<br />2.	The writing, however, is not perfect, but the story is. I love the people of Carnal Colorado with all their quirky kinks and kinky quirks. Hippies, stalkers, alchies, and killers, adorable kids, annoying exes and bikers out the ying-yang... <i>Sweet Dreams</i> has it all. It’s about 15 million pages long - give or take - but it’s still too short. <br />	<br />3. 	It’s hot, it’s sexy, it’s dirty, but it’s such a great love story, in a biker kinda way. One of my favorite lines in the book is when Tate tells Lauren, <i> “I get back, Lauren, you’re on the back of my bike.”</i>*sigh* So romantic!</blockquote>So there ya have it, a few of the reason I love this story and didn’t want it to end. I hope you’ll give these books a try so you can discover for yourself what an amazing series it is.<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /><br /><br /></span>

    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/820331144?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer820331144" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4992464341487527418"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 1/11/2014) </i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Review Re-Read 6/8/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 9/10/2018) - Still one of my faves and a good re-read 🤗</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 6/3/2019) - Ths remains my reliable re-read when I'm having troubles connecting in other books</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This has to be my favorite KA book and my favorite book to re-read period, and I can't believe I've never written a review for it! Is it the best book I've read? No. But it never fails in making me feel good -- and that's</span>
  <span id="freeText4992464341487527418" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 1/11/2014) </i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Review Re-Read 6/8/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 9/10/2018) - Still one of my faves and a good re-read 🤗</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 6/3/2019) - Ths remains my reliable re-read when I'm having troubles connecting in other books</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This has to be my favorite KA book and my favorite book to re-read period, and I can't believe I've never written a review for it! Is it the best book I've read? No. But it never fails in making me feel good -- and that's why we read books, right?! <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> is always my go-to when I'm in need for some good closure and a HEA. This book is not the best ending she's written, but it still gives me that smile on my face when I get to the end. AND...I just love Tate so darn much! I am incredibly happy to report that he is everything I love in KA heroes even after a re-read! I was truly worried he wouldn't hold up...especially after being so disappointed in myself after re-reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_" title="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a> and Tack not being the man I had in my head the second go-round. It's no secret that I am not a huge fan of suspense in romance, but this book has just the right balance between romance/suspense/other stuff to keep me interested and eating up the super long book in no time! <br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lauren and Tate's story. Lauren is on the road trying to find herself a new home after a devistating divorce, and she lands herself in a small town in the Colorado mountains. She gets a waitressing job at the local bar, and she starts to plant her roots by making new friends and finally being herself. She meets Tate, who is a part owner of the bar, and they bump heads right away. When a serial killed hits too close to home, things between them change drastically. There is a good bit of ex drama (on both ends), some big secrets revealed, some friend and family drama, some sexy times, AND a serial killer on the loose...but they do eventually get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told primarily in Lauren's POV with a few sections in other character's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. This is another long one! On Amazon it is listed at 678 pages. I never have issues getting through it though, because SO many things happen! I never skimmed, and it flows well throughout.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a while to develop stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4.75 😜 stars. Tate. My #1 all time favorite KA hero. That's not so say he doesn't get OTT in his alpha jerkish ways at times, but I just can't help falling for him every time I read this.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Lauren. I like her. Yes -- she is a little clueless at times, but I loved how she took care of her boys.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I teared up a few times, but never needed any tissues. I have re-read this several times, and I think I remember tearing up more with those first reads.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h holds a mean grudge and pushes away at first. The H is the main pursuer of the relationship. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Hot. They have some hot tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I don't remember any mention of birth control, std statuses, or previous practices.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Both the h and H's exes cause a good bit of drama. There is also another man vying for the h's attention.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[But the h sees the H for the first time when he is making out and going into a hotel room with an OW.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Not IMO <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ See below regarding first separation -- to me it didn't feel like cheating, but I can see where others might think so. The H did have an affair with a married OW before the h. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for about a month. There was no mention or suggestion of the H having other partners during this time because he thought he was with the h, but the h was with OM during this time (not intercourse but "fooling around") because she was unaware that the H thought they were together (and other things). There are a few more times that they are separated physically, but no other partners during these times.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h is recently divorced and her ex cheated on her with her best friend (off page), the H was carrying on an affair with an OW that was married to an OM (on page for one non-descriptive scene) before the h, rape/physical assault/murder/attempted murder/kidnapping of side characters serial killer (off page but some details), kidnapping/attempted murder (on page), and H has child with OW (on page). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This has great closure with a jump ahead epilogue and a HEA. KA does endings the way I like!!<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid $3.98 for it on Amazon back in 2014.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably <u>Safe with exception </u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating (see above)<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a few separations between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse by mcs<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="4992464341487527418" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/396575923?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/23278796-sweet-dreams">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=best-of-the-bestest">best-of-the-bestest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396575923" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6151252164370349710"><b>Re-re-read April 13, 2018</b><br/><br/>Tate - "Do you love me?"<br/><br/>Laurie - "Yes"<br/><br/>Tate - "That's it"<br/><br/>Yes Tate, that is it. Geez, I love this audio. No change on my rating, just wish I could add bonus stars for re-reads.<br/><br/>****<br/><br/><b>Re-read July 7, 2017</b><br/><br/>That re-read never gets old. Tate is still one of my FAVOURITE macho alpha male heroes who is far from perfect but still manages to make my heart swoon.<br/><br/>What's a girl to do? Move on to a re-read of Lady Luck, of course. :-)<br/><br/>****<br/><br/><b>Baking day became something to look forward to...</b><br/><br/>I </span>
  <span id="freeText6151252164370349710" style="display:none"><b>Re-re-read April 13, 2018</b><br /><br />Tate - "Do you love me?"<br /><br />Laurie - "Yes"<br /><br />Tate - "That's it"<br /><br />Yes Tate, that is it. Geez, I love this audio. No change on my rating, just wish I could add bonus stars for re-reads.<br /><br />****<br /><br /><b>Re-read July 7, 2017</b><br /><br />That re-read never gets old. Tate is still one of my FAVOURITE macho alpha male heroes who is far from perfect but still manages to make my heart swoon.<br /><br />What's a girl to do? Move on to a re-read of Lady Luck, of course. :-)<br /><br />****<br /><br /><b>Baking day became something to look forward to...</b><br /><br />I have read Sweet Dreams a few times...any real KA fan has. When the audio version became available I snapped it up and couldn't wait to get started.<br /><br />Tate, as KA heroes go, is up there with the best. A strong, virile and attractive man who knows what he wants, goes after it and takes no prisoners until he gets it. He doesn't show himself off in the most flattering way when he meets Laurie for the first time, and TBH I was devastated the first time I read it. I couldn't see how he'd redeem himself after the hurtful things he said. Luckily, my faith in this author was strong, so I settled in to see how and what he does to make things better.<br /><br />Laurie is getting over divorcing her douchewaffle ex when she hits Carnal and decides to settle for a while. She approaches the local bar and meets Crys the part owner/manager who eventually gives her a chance. Laurie settles in well and makes lots of friends.<br /><br />Tate and Laurie together are smoking hot. We see their feelings grow for each other which helps them deal with the storms heading their way. Both Laurie and Tate have ex's that don't want to let go. Laurie has to deal with a family member getting sick. Tate has work and family commitments and there's a serial killer on the loose.<br /><br />I really enjoyed the audio version. The narrator does a wonderful job of changing her voice to suit each character and it was clear when each change happened. I sometimes feel the story more with audio. In this case I definitely did. I was sniggering, sniffling and snorting out loud enough to draw my family's attention. I had to remind myself numerous times that my nine and twelve year old sons couldn't hear the foul language or the sex scenes that were making me squirm.<br /><br />Most of my listening was done while I baked. This gives me double the pleasure. I love to bake for my family and I love to read/listen to Kristen Ashley. I don't think I will ever tire of Sweet Dreams. Tate and Laurie together in Carnal, always leaves me with a smile on my face.<br /><br />This review and more can be found at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://edgyreviews.com/">http://edgyreviews.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6151252164370349710" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_245570384" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/245570384" />
    <a title=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida"><img alt=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1295034921p2/1453659.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/245570384?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" href="/user/show/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida"> Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=owned-read">owned-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=romance-contemporary">romance-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245570384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer777508938780555799">(Edited to add more sexy Tate pics)<br/><br/><b>4 Stars</b> - <b>
  <i>Also reviewed at: <a href='http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-sweet-dreams-by-kristen-ashley.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a></i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Sweet Dreams</i>
</b> didn’t just have “Moist Factor Five Hundred”, for me, it had the “Turn Around Factor”.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716486.gif' width='170' height='220' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In fact, it even made me feel like I was doing the Twister!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716487._SX540_.gif' width='220' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Why do I say this? Weeelll…. I was initially quite drawn into this story DESPITE its editing issues. <br/><br/>Yes, this book has overly long/run-on sentences; under-use of commas and full stops; over-use of parentheses; and some non-linear time lines. If y</span>
  <span id="freeText777508938780555799" style="display:none">(Edited to add more sexy Tate pics)<br><br><b>4 Stars</b> - <b>
  <i>Also reviewed at: <a href="http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-sweet-dreams-by-kristen-ashley.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a></i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Sweet Dreams</i>
</b> didn’t just have “Moist Factor Five Hundred”, for me, it had the “Turn Around Factor”.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716486.gif" width="170" height="220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In fact, it even made me feel like I was doing the Twister!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716487._SX540_.gif" width="220" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why do I say this? Weeelll…. I was initially quite drawn into this story DESPITE its editing issues. <br><br>Yes, this book has overly long/run-on sentences; under-use of commas and full stops; over-use of parentheses; and some non-linear time lines. If you are a reader who can’t get passed this, then this book is not for you. This is a self-published book.<br><br>Despite noticing all these issues, though, it really didn’t bother me because, as I said, I was drawn into the story. It’s been said before, but I concur: Kristen Ashley is a great storyteller and has great characterisations. Her characters seemed so real. In fact, <i>that</i> is really where my main issue arose (which I’ll explain more later).<br><br>The story is written in first person POV of Lauren Grahame, a newly divorced 42-year old woman from middle class suburbia in search of “Nowheresville”. Lauren used to believe in “something special” but her cheating husband changed all that. She no longer expected “special” and wanted to escape into a nothing place, never thinking that Carnal, Colorado, a small biker town, would ever be home or where she would indeed find “special”. <br><br>Lauren was an extremely likable and relatable character. She is sweet, caring, gets along with almost anyone, a hard worker, classy, but she's also insecure, and well, can be quite impulsive and reckless. <br><br>I want to say THANK YOU to all my Goodreads friends who first encouraged me to read it and also to “Hang in There” with this book! The story was well worth my time despite pushing some very personal buttons. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716488._SY540_.jpg" width="220" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, on to the hard part… What <i>were</i> my personal buttons? Hmm…Well, it was Tate Jackson who pushed them. It is something that upsets me to talk/write/think about, but to fully explain my issue with Tate, I feel I need to share.<br><br>I wasn’t just annoyed with Tate. I was MAD at him. The introduction to Tate isn’t the best. Though, that wasn’t even my main issue. <br><br>Tate is bossy and controlling. Yes, he’s an alpha male, and maybe at a different point in my life I might have been less upset by this. Recent events, though, made me really angry seeing this behaviour in Tate. My dad has always been the “boss” of the family. But in the last few years he has developed a brain condition that is causing his motor abilities to degenerate, such that a man of only 65 can’t walk without the aid of a walker, and it will just get worse. What really breaks my heart, though, is what I would have formerly seen as just protective behaviour by my dad, has become over-possessive and controlling behaviour. This behaviour has always been there. It is just so much worse now. It is such that my mum can’t even speak to <i>me</i> on the phone without him needing to be present, because he is paranoid she is planning to run away with a young lover. This is not the case. My mum is faithful and does everything for him. He is constantly bossing her around and she isn’t even allowed to sleep with her back to him because then her “body language” is all wrong. I love both my mum and dad and it really breaks my heart. I feel all teary now just thinking about it.<br><br>Also, Lauren’s nickname for Tate was “Captain” and my dad was a ship’s captain and everyone calls him that, even mum when she’s talking about him to others.<br><br>Anyway, these feelings about my dad is something that’s very difficult for me to deal with, and seeing Tate’s controlling and bossy behaviour (as well as some annoying repetitions in text)…well…I needed to step away from this book, for a bit. I was almost considering "DNF"-ing it. <br><br>I decided to re-read an emotional favourite of mine, <b>
  <i>The Bronze Horseman</i>
</b>, because I needed to hurt. I needed to cry, without necessarily thinking about my mum and dad. <br><br>After I released some of these emotions, I decided to go back and continue <i>
  <b>Sweet Dreams</b>
</i> and I was completely sucked into the story. I can completely understand now how my GRs friends couldn’t put this one down. <br><br>Only several pages in from where I stepped away, I was met with this scene below. It made a big dent in melting my heart.<blockquote>
  <i>“And he cradled it, the cat’s lower body resting on his forearm, the cat’s tail gliding across his bicep, the cat’s front paws straddling Tate’s wrist and the cat’s head resting in Tate’s big hand.”</i>
</blockquote>Tell me that an image something like this doesn’t melt your heart, too? Aaww<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www">www</a>..…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716489._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although, Buster looks more like this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379763165i/217202.jpg" width="350" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I LOVED Buster! She was a real present character. Being owned by a cat, myself, her behaviours were just soooo adorably <i>cat</i>, to me. ^_^<br><br>Back to Tate...In the end, in spite of Tate still being such a jerk, at times – especially, when he’s pissed off or because he is just being his “bossy” self – I ended up loving him. Tate does some very thoughtful and sweet things, in his very Tate way. He doesn’t make my Top heroes list, but as my friend Jill said, he is an “unforgettable hero”. <br><br>I like how Lauren argues with him. She doesn’t take it lying down…well, sometimes she does, if you know what I mean . ^_~ *snickers*.<br><br>I know that Tate will still do things to frustrate and annoy me – we all have people like that in our lives, and yet we still love them – but he’s a good man and he and Lauren really do bring out the best in each other. I love how he spoiled her, how he made her see what “special” is, and taught her to see herself through his eyes –YOWZA! If only I’d had “treatment” like that for my anorexia and insomnia! *fans self* LOL<br><br>See, I’m writing about him like he’s REAL! Kudos to Ms Ashley on characterisation!<br><br>Also, there was an amazing and interesting cast of "secondary" characters! Loved Shambles and Sunny, Betty and Ned, Jim-Billy, Wendy, Krystal, Wood, Jonas, and Laurie's family!<br><br>I was kept on the edge of my seat with the suspense elements. <br><br>I even enjoyed reading about what Lauren was wearing almost every day; but then again, I like clothes, as does, it seems, Ms Ashley, from what I read in the “About the Author” portion of the book<br><br>So, for the “Turn Around Factor”, I’m giving this one 4 Stars.<br><br>Tate…He can be such a <i>jerk</i>, but he has his oh-so-sweet moments, and, man, he’s gorgeous!<blockquote>
  <i>“He was tall, maybe taller than he seemed in the parking lot or maybe he just seemed bigger in the bar since his shoulders were so broad. But his hips were lean and his legs were long, his thighs obviously powerfully muscled and I could tell that through his jeans. His dark brown hair gleamed even in the dull light of the bar. It was thick and it was clear he washed it and let it fall where it lay for the part was natural and not straight, it was swept back but some fell around his temples and curled a bit around his ears and at the back of his neck. His eyes looked dark. I couldn’t tell the color but there were sun lines emanating from the sides that were attractive. His brow was heavy; his nose wasn’t perfect but it was straight with a slight bump at the top of the bridge that made it interesting; his cheekbones were cut and his jaw was strong. His skin was tanned in a way where I knew he didn’t get that color lounging by the pool and he was wearing faded jeans, black motorcycle boots and a heathered-gray-blue, long-sleeved, skintight, thermal Henley.<br>He was beautiful.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379764906i/232266._SY540_.jpg" width="310" height="460" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>Tate looks HOT in a Henley...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716490.jpg" width="400" height="440" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>...And without one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716491.jpg" width="350" height="460" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He's a badass biker and bounty hunter...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364708i/716492.jpg" width="340" height="460" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>...And he's a yummy playmate in the pool.</i>
</b><br><br><br><i>DISCLAIMER: I do not hold the copyright to any of the images used in this review. They are posted to add visuals to the review and for fun. If any of these images are yours and you would like me to remove them, please let me know, and I will do so as soon as possible. If I can identify the copyright, I will do so.</i><br></span>

<div id="review_3550522495" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3550522495" />
    <a title="Phuong ✯" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32821952-phuong"><img alt="Phuong ✯" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568488671p2/32821952.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3550522495?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer10672599288227750971">– <b>
  <i>4.25 stars</i>
</b><br/><br/>KA's books just work for me. I love the heroine, I love the Hero, I love their romance, I love the kids, I love the friendships, I love the family moments ... they are comfort. I love reading about the characters cooking, doing BBQs, buying curtains and being all domestic with e/o. That gives me so much pleasure LOL. <br/><br/>All of her books (maybe besides <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12458287.The_Golden_Dynasty__Fantasyland___2_' title='The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Golden Dynasty</a>) follow the same pattern and have very similar tropes, so I can understand why it can get boring for some, but I l</span>
  <span id="freeText10672599288227750971" style="display:none">– <b>
  <i>4.25 stars</i>
</b><br /><br />KA's books just work for me. I love the heroine, I love the Hero, I love their romance, I love the kids, I love the friendships, I love the family moments ... they are comfort. I love reading about the characters cooking, doing BBQs, buying curtains and being all domestic with e/o. That gives me so much pleasure LOL. <br /><br />All of her books (maybe besides <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12458287.The_Golden_Dynasty__Fantasyland___2_" title="The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Golden Dynasty</a>) follow the same pattern and have very similar tropes, so I can understand why it can get boring for some, but I love it. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"You said you were waiting' for something special and he took away your chance to figure out that you were carrying' it with you all this time. You are special Laurie."</b>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_639131387" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639131387" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639131387?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">KA Fans, Romance, Everyone</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17755575-wendy-sthoughts?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639131387" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5955933600534675328"><b>5 Tate Induced Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free-2018/2014 Re-Read</i><br/><b><i> Re-Read for the Umpteenth Time. Recently started the series again and am working my way through. Since I first read the books in 2013, some do not have reviews. This one does. </i></b><br/>**************************************<br/>One of the main reasons I figured out how to get the Amazon App for PC was to read Kristen Ashley. I was new to romance and discovered many authors I loved. I found their books at Goodwill and dollar bookstores at reduced pri</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5955933600534675328" style="display:none"><b>5 Tate Induced Stars<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free-2018/2014 Re-Read</i><br><b><i> Re-Read for the Umpteenth Time. Recently started the series again and am working my way through. Since I first read the books in 2013, some do not have reviews. This one does. </i></b><br>**************************************<br>One of the main reasons I figured out how to get the Amazon App for PC was to read Kristen Ashley. I was new to romance and discovered many authors I loved. I found their books at Goodwill and dollar bookstores at reduced prices once I discovered them from my shopping at the brick and mortar Barnes and Noble. You see libraries didn't work for me. I finally came to that conclusion after admitting to myself I had issues with returning on time... <br><br>After joining Goodreads and seeing all the comments about KA's books, I figured out how to acquire them.... and her books were the first ebooks I bought.<br><br>Sweet Dreams.... really is just that. KA takes real-life issues we confront and wraps them in emotionally triggered dreams of what things could be if we meet people who foster them for us. <br><br>All of us can feel less than, not worthy of a partner...all of us can feel we are never going to accomplish a goal or have what we hoped for. We may have worked towards something and then either because of circumstances beyond our control lose it, or maybe we give up not due to fear of failure but due to deep-rooted fear of success which reflects back to us not thinking we are worth it.<br><br>These are only some of the issues addressed in this book. What was so interesting as I re-read this was how very deep the level of interpersonal relationships went... how KA presented such serious things wrapped in a way which almost could be considered throw away...<br><br>She would have her characters bicker or banter... and then cut to the underlining meaning of it all... self-discovery aided by eyes of another. The person would figure things out for themselves... but through their development of the relationship with their love interest; each needing each other to achieve a goal never really intended... but clear to us as readers... <br><br>Although KA's style of writing takes some getting used to... once you do... it becomes like that old sweatshirt you wear when you want comfort; that thing which just grounds you. There is no specific reason except... you feel safe and good.</b><br><br>In this book, Tate, the GUY.... is a GUY. No metro-sexual; just a testosterone god who reeks Man... and we love him.<br><br>We love his asshole ways because even though they are annoying... he will say he was... own up to it and want to move on. He has no room for grudges. He will do what he says he is going to do and lives up to his promises. He cares about those around him. But the best... the real best... he has no problem with showing affection. Nope... he doesn't give a shit... if he wants to kiss his woman, he does... and often. He likes to make sure others are aware she is his... with arms wrapped around her... but mostly not for show... it is because in the moments he feels the need to do it. It is a wonder... and that can be a sweet dream.<br><br>Her other main character is Lauren and she has reached a point in her life... she thinks is to just live... exist and not expect anything "special". She thought it was out there... had betrayal, lies, and disappointment instead. She is lost but doesn't know it. <br><br>These two connect and it is a perfect catalyst for KA to present everything she has on her mind. <br><br>This is a terrific story of people coming together... learning about themselves while learning about each other. The characters are complex; the community is full and has depth. You become involved and want to know what will happen from the start.<br><br>KA knew what she wanted to say; she had issues she wanted to present with real feelings of how to work them out. She figured out a plan; made it happen and got the results. I love how she did it and actually am thrilled she did. Her concepts and ways of taking these issues to those who experience them worked. Plus.... we got Tate and that is always a good thing.<br><br>Sweet Dreams is the second in the Colorado Series. I personally feel some of her best writing is in this series and the Burg series. They are meaty... with people living everyday lives...<br>(well sort of- Tate is a Bounty Hunter) and are in the throws of learning to love again. They belong to communities, surrounded by those who either have loved them well or have caused great pain. They are us and sometimes watching and learning how these people grow can make us feel we can too.<br><br>So, I will continue to throw on that worn sweatshirt I love... the one that makes me feel safe and good... and look for my next KA story.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1327890208l/11227041._SX50_.jpg" alt="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth"><img alt="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558713329p2/7420520.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1340052174?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" href="/user/show/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth">Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1340052174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13564842484254851020">✮✮✮ ALL THE STARS ✮✮✮<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495956896i/22870288._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a href='https://vanillaandspicebooks.blogspot.com/2017/08/5-stars-kristen-ashley-sweet-dreams.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review @ Vanilla & Spice Books</a><br/><br/><br/><b>Re-read - July 2017</b><br/><br/><br/>Fat.<br/>Old.<br/>Sorry-ass.<br/>Choice words her new boss Tate Jackson has for Lauren. After months on the road looking for a place she'd want to stay she arrives in Carnal, Colorado. A former exec, she starts working as a waitress at Bubba's, a biker bar. When she overhears Tate insulting her she is hurt. She is done letting people like her ex-husband walk over her, she's done adapting to other people's whims and moods. She throws attitude</span>
  <span id="freeText13564842484254851020" style="display:none">✮✮✮ ALL THE STARS ✮✮✮<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495956896i/22870288._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://vanillaandspicebooks.blogspot.com/2017/08/5-stars-kristen-ashley-sweet-dreams.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review @ Vanilla &amp; Spice Books</a><br><br><br><b>Re-read - July 2017</b><br><br><br>Fat.<br>Old.<br>Sorry-ass.<br>Choice words her new boss Tate Jackson has for Lauren. After months on the road looking for a place she'd want to stay she arrives in Carnal, Colorado. A former exec, she starts working as a waitress at Bubba's, a biker bar. When she overhears Tate insulting her she is hurt. She is done letting people like her ex-husband walk over her, she's done adapting to other people's whims and moods. She throws attitude in Tate's beautiful face and holds on to her mammoth grudge.<br><br>Tate, bounty hunter/bar keeper and owner/ex-cop/ex-pro-football player, was sure that Lauren Grahame wouldn't fit into his bar. Too high-class, too pretty, too much of everything. But still, her hair, her legs, her attitude and pretty face, it all draws him to her. She has the attention of the local bikers and is popular with the bar's crowd. He knows when he comes back from chasing a skip he wants her on the back of his bike. When a serial killer makes a re-appearance in Carnal Tate's need to protect Laurie becomes his focus.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It isn't that it's too soon, you're on the back of my bike, it ain't too soon. You can buy sheets. You cannot install blinds."<br>"um..." I mumbled. "Can you explain the difference?"<br>"Sheets are chick territory," he said without delay. "You gotta use tools, that's dick territory."<br>"Oh," I whispered.<br>"Don't tread on dick territory," he advised.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489734970i/22243857._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Nobody in the book world, NOBODY writes alpha males better than Kristen Ashley. Tate is my guy, he is and has always been my favorite KA-hero. That being said, I am not through with her back list, yet so who knows!<br><br>Tate is a bossy, over-protective and possessive guy and many times you just want to kick him because he has a temper that turns him into an asshole. But the good outweighs that by far. He has a sweet that is irresistible, is resolute and strong-willed.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“His forehead dropped to touch mine. “I’m gonna piss you off ‘cause I can be a dick. That’s who I am. And you’re gonna piss me off ‘cause, babe, you got attitude. That’s who you are. And that’s who we’re comin’ out to be together. And I’m all right with that because, with what I had before, even when you’re a bitch, I like it. But when you’re not, it’s a sweetness the like I’ve never tasted.” <br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>He sets his sight on something, he goes after it, no holds barred. I loved that you never had to guess his feelings, they were always out there even though the story was mostly written from Laurie's POV.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Two kinds of women get under your skin. The ones who do damage, they don't feel good there but once you're fuckin' stupid enough to let them in you got no choice but to take the time it takes to work them out. Then there are the ones who don't do damage, who feel good there, feed the muscle, the bone, the soul, not rip it or break it or burn it. The ones you don't wanna work out.” - Tate<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Yeah, that Tate Jackson is so amazing because he is flawed. Also, his relationship with his son is so sweet, the way a man treats his son? When it's that sweet it you can bid farewell to your ovaries.<br><br>Laurie is a wonderful character. She has that vibe that whatever bothers you, whatever you need you can count on her. She has that open personality that draws people in and makes them do things for her to please her. But she is also stubborn and that is where she locks horns with Tate, because that guy has invented stubborn. Laurie can also hold a grudge like no other and spends a lot of time in her head when she does. I loved how she paid attention to the people she loved.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489734970i/22243857._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sweet Dreams has everything, humor, suspense, romance in tons and lovable main and side characters. And Jesus, Tate's dirty mouth...*fans herself*<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You buy me sheets. You paint my room. What's next? You gonna wash my balls?" -Tate</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This is - so far - my favorite Kristen Ashley book and I've read a lot by this author. Every single one of her stories has a special place in my heart but this one is on a pedestal. I have it on good authority that At Peace from Ms Ashley's The Burg series might contest that spot! We'll see.<br><br>Sweet Dreams is the second installment of the Colorado Mountain series and can be read as a standalone.<br><br><br><a href="http://coffeecookieandbooks.blogspot.co.at/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1486060125i/21877446._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/VanillaandSpiceBooks/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491980409i/22468566.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7420520-astrid" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491980409i/22468570.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/VanSpicebooks" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491980409i/22468568.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.instagram.com/vanillaandspicebooks/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491980409i/22468567.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1561125332" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1561125332" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1561125332?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23785504-sweet-dreams">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1561125332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16484938683969201896">This is a typical KA-land book where the alpha males shift from super sweet to semi-jerky at the drop of a hat…but all in an I’m a man and I’m going to provide and protect you kind of way. This is a place where normal rules don’t apply really. <br/><br/><b>Things to Expect in KA-Land</b><br/><br/>❣ - Ex’s are 5 shades of cray-cray and I mean CrAzY<br/><br/>❣ - The Hot guy will say something life shattering sweet one minute and then act like he is from another time the next and you’ll want to first kiss him and then kick him in the </span>
  <span id="freeText16484938683969201896" style="display:none">This is a typical KA-land book where the alpha males shift from super sweet to semi-jerky at the drop of a hat…but all in an I’m a man and I’m going to provide and protect you kind of way. This is a place where normal rules don’t apply really. <br /><br /><b>Things to Expect in KA-Land</b><br /><br />❣ - Ex’s are 5 shades of cray-cray and I mean CrAzY<br /><br />❣ - The Hot guy will say something life shattering sweet one minute and then act like he is from another time the next and you’ll want to first kiss him and then kick him in the balls. That feeling goes a little back and forth but most of the stuff that is memorable is sweet.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Two kinds of women get under your skin. The ones who do damage, they don't feel good there but once you're fuckin' stupid enough to let them in you got no choice but to take the time it takes to work them out. Then there are the ones who don't do damage, who feel good there, feed the muscle, the bone, the soul, not rip it or break it or burn it. The ones you don't wanna work out.” </i>
</blockquote><br />❣ - The underappreciated girl with a past will resist the initial allure of said hot guy because she has something tragic in her past or is slightly broken. But at least she is not 20 something….<b>One of the best things about KAs MCs is that most of the time they are in their 30s and 40s.</b><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“All my life, or as long as I can remember, I thought something special was going to happen to me. I just had this feeling, deep in my bones. I didn’t know what it was but it was going to be beautiful, spectacular, huge.” I leaned in further. “All… my… life.” I shook my head again and put my hand on the bar. “It didn’t. I waited and it didn’t happen. I waited more and it didn’t happen. I waited more and it still didn’t happen. I tried to make it happen and it still didn’t happen. Now I know it isn’t going to. It’s never going to happen because there isn’t anything special out there to happen.”</i>
</blockquote><br />❣ - The KA heroine will freak out at some point and time and ramble on in a cute or over informative way.<br /><br />❣ - There will be sex…lots of hot sex…even some in the shower and <i>that is when I know this isn’t real life. Because have you ever tried to have sex in the shower…it is slippery and I think you are more likely to get a concussion than an orgasm</i><br /><br />❣ - At some point there will be some crass talk…I personally look forward to this. It is usually dirty and mostly thrown in the face of someone who has wronged the MC so I totally look forward to the verbal smack down. There were a few of them in Sweet Dreams and they were all awesome.<br /><br />❣ - You can usually count on a kidnapping, girl fight, alpha dominance fight or a tasering. If you are lucky you get a combo of them.<br /><br /><b>Sweet Dreams worked for me for a few reasons.</b> I liked Laurie most of the time. She had a bad marriage and is a bit gun shy but she stands up for herself doesn’t let anyone walk all over her and is good to her friends. There is also Tate who made me happy just a little more than he made me angry but overall he just did it for me. It was probably all the crass talking.<br /><br />The murder mystery while interesting totally plays second fiddle to the love story. This IS love story first and foremost with a mystery. Still I always love learning about the pasts of the characters to see why they are both a little broken and each one helps to fix the other. Tate’s history was just as tragic as Laurie’s was but in a different way.<br /><br />KA did fortunately reign in all of the descriptions in this one. There are still a lot and I always know what a character is wearing, or the general vibe of a room but she didn’t go nearly as overboard as she did in The Gamble. <br /><br />The side characters and the small town always add a lot to the story and this is no exception. I love that I feel like these are real places and you could go and visit Carnal and have a drink at Bubba’s and run in to Jim-Billy there and maybe watch Twyla throw down some attitude at bad tipping customers. <br /><br />All and all this is one of my favorite KA books to date.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16484938683969201896" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_275339848" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/275339848" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/275339848?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer275339848" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17198015620861592508"><b><br/>Re-read June 4, 2018<br/>Re-read May 31, 2017. </b><br/><br/>This was my first Kristen Ashley book and it was just as good if not better the second time around. Since then I've read several of her books, but Sweet Dreams continues to be one of my all-time KA favorites. I've changed my 4 star rating to a 5 star, because I only rated down because of all the typos in her original self-published edition. Since then those have been corrected, and I love her signature rambling, run-on sentences, so I'm glad that wasn't </span>
  <span id="freeText17198015620861592508" style="display:none"><b><br />Re-read June 4, 2018<br />Re-read May 31, 2017. </b><br /><br />This was my first Kristen Ashley book and it was just as good if not better the second time around. Since then I've read several of her books, but Sweet Dreams continues to be one of my all-time KA favorites. I've changed my 4 star rating to a 5 star, because I only rated down because of all the typos in her original self-published edition. Since then those have been corrected, and I love her signature rambling, run-on sentences, so I'm glad that wasn't changed. <br /><b><br />Original review from 2012:</b><br />Forty-two year-old, Lauren's "picture perfect" marriage, of ten years, has fallen apart. She found out her husband, Brad, has been having an affair with her best friend for the last five years. Ouch! Lauren wants to escape the privileged life and her so-called friends (they all knew of the affair). So she's been on a road trip for four months but wants to finally settle somewhere. So she's decided to find a nowhere town and find a nowhere job, not to find anything "special" but to find peace. She ends up in Carnal, Colorado at a biker bar called Bubba's, and snags a job as a waitress. Lauren takes residence in the local motel and starts making friends. This is where she spots beautiful biker-man, Tate, pull up on his Harley and meet up with a larger than life woman, Neeta. Little does she know that this beyond hot man is one of her bosses at Bubba's bar. She shows up for work the next day and Tate walks in. Let's just put it this way. These two do NOT hit it off at first. Tate says something, almost unforgivable, about Lauren, and she overhears. Needless to say, these two lock heads for a while but there is obvious chemistry. Things begin to change when there's a murder and everyone is on alert. For some reason, beyond the understanding of Lauren, Tate makes Lauren's safety his priority. <br /><br />I loved this book! Tate was alpha-male at its finest! He was possessive and protective. He could be rude and gruff, but his underlying loyalty and sweetness completely won me over! Plus, tattooed, hot biker guy, who can resist? I loved Lauren's character as well. To see her transformation from insecure and lost, to strong and confident was enjoyable. I was rooting for her at every step. She was such a sweetie, and her personal interest in everyone in the town, won them over to the point of everyone loving her. Everyone that is, except for Neeta, the woman we first see Tate with. Thankfully, Tate won't allow her to cause too many problems, but boy that woman was a hot mess! <br /><br />You may have seen reviews on this book with people complaining of the typos, punctuation and run-on-sentence issues. This is true. This author is self-published and unfortunately, the editing is not what it could be. If this sort of thing annoys you to the point of ruining a story, you'd be better off passing on this one. But if you can overlook these issues, I highly recommend this book. The story was addictive and touching. The mystery surrounding the killings was good too, I was guessing up to the very end. I will be reading the rest of the books in the Colorado Mountain series. Kristen Ashley has found a fan in me!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17198015620861592508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_318285330" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/318285330" />
    <a title="Susan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/739211-susan"><img alt="Susan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1335133091p2/739211.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/318285330?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susan" href="/user/show/739211-susan">Susan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer318285330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6089803947752089179"><br/><b>REREAD (April 10, 2015)</b><br/><br/>In a time where I've grown less patient w/ overly long books, less-than-tight editing, and generic romances...<br/><br/>I'm kinda shocked to find that I STILL LOVE THIS BOOK as much as I did the first and second times reading it! For some reason, Tate and Laurie stand the test of time for me. Their love story is EVERYTHING! And I ended it, again, in pure bliss. <br/><br/>Three years later, almost to the day, since I finsihed it the first time...and still my favorite KA book...<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>REREAD (May 15, </b></span>
  <span id="freeText6089803947752089179" style="display:none"><br /><b>REREAD (April 10, 2015)</b><br /><br />In a time where I've grown less patient w/ overly long books, less-than-tight editing, and generic romances...<br /><br />I'm kinda shocked to find that I STILL LOVE THIS BOOK as much as I did the first and second times reading it! For some reason, Tate and Laurie stand the test of time for me. Their love story is EVERYTHING! And I ended it, again, in pure bliss. <br /><br />Three years later, almost to the day, since I finsihed it the first time...and still my favorite KA book...<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>REREAD (May 15, 2013)</b><br /><br />This was my first KA book I'd ever read and I loved it the first time. After reading 20+ more of her books, along with 100's more other books since then, this remains one of my FAVORITE romance books...EVER.<br /><br />Rereading it was a TREAT. I savored it. I normally power read through books. But with this, I read chapters, allowed myself to smile, fantasized a little bit about Tate, hugged my kindle, and then went back to reading. It was a joy. <br /><br /><u>New Observation:</u><br />I loved Tate the first time. I LOVED TATE the second time. Man, that guy is...just...just...THE BEST. His first words still stung, maybe even more this time around. But, sheesh, if a man can make up for hurt feelings like he does...whooooo wheeeee. God he redeems himself SO HARD. LOVE HIM!<br /><br /><b>Original rating: 5 stars<br />Reread rating: 5 stars</b><br /><br />***********************************<br /><br /><b>ORIGINAL REVIEW (April 12, 2012)</b><br /><br />I kinda loved this book. <br /><br />1. Lauren is the BEST heroine in any chick-lit/romance book I've ever read! (yes, even I'd want her on the back of my bike...if I rode a bike...and had such inclinations). AND, I want her to be my best friend. <br /><br />2. The scene w/ Wanda at the home goods store when Lauren &amp; Wendy are buying sheets is PRICELESS. Pure comedy. <br /><br />3. Secret's out: Jim-Billy is the true leading man in this book. :)<br /><br />Reading this book made me want to savor every page and I literally laughed, cried, worried, and celebrated w/ the characters.<br /><br />Question: why do all of these books seem to have angry, hard, oftentimes-mean leading men? Is that what every author really thinks women want? (and secretly do they?) I know we all want the Jerry McGuire "You complete me" fairy tale and to save a man from himself...but to put up with some of the anger issues...I don't know if it's worth it.<br /><br />That being said, I'm not trying to hate on Tate. I actually heart him. I just think the angry alpha-male could get old real-quick. (luckily the book ended before it got old)<br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="6089803947752089179" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_261710322" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/261710322" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/261710322?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of hot contemporary romance</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Auntee by: </span>
      Viv
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=for_my_kindle">for_my_kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2012_reads">2012_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer261710322" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5671271959314327476">There's already 159(!) reviews of this book, so I doubt that I have anything to add that hasn't already been said. So I'll give just a few impressions...<br/><br/>Kristen Ashley, you're a fabulous writer. Great storyteller. You create sigh-worthy heroes and spunky heroines. I love your dialogue. Your love scenes are smokin' hot, passionate, and convincing. I'm a detail junkie and I love details, and you provide in spades. <br/><br/>However...there is such a thing as too much of a good thing. <i>Sweet Dreams</i> is <b>loaded</b> </span>
  <span id="freeText5671271959314327476" style="display:none">There's already 159(!) reviews of this book, so I doubt that I have anything to add that hasn't already been said. So I'll give just a few impressions...<br><br>Kristen Ashley, you're a fabulous writer. Great storyteller. You create sigh-worthy heroes and spunky heroines. I love your dialogue. Your love scenes are smokin' hot, passionate, and convincing. I'm a detail junkie and I love details, and you provide in spades. <br><br>However...there is such a thing as too much of a good thing. <i>Sweet Dreams</i> is <b>loaded</b> with details, and for the first 250 pages or so, that was fine with me. But (*gasp*) there was a time where I was tempted to skim! Around the time that Laurie and Tate were getting along just fine and you knew they were on the road to everlasting love, the story got a little bogged down in the details (what Laurie was wearing, baking, or buying) and I just wanted the story to move forward. I wanted them to find out who the serial killer was already!<br><br>But I didn't skim, and that was because I didn't want to miss anything about Tate. What a studtastic hero! Laurie was one lucky woman...<br><br>So other than the excess length of this book, I thought it was wonderful. The plotting, the characters, the nicknames ("Ace" and "Captain"), the love scenes (plenty HAWT, but not so much to bog down the book), even the suspense plot...all first rate. And badass biker, bar owner, bounty hunter, ex-police detective and ex-NFL linebacker Tate, even though he put the "M" in macho, had a temper, sometimes said wildly inappropriate things...I thought he was totally swoonworthy, and I believed 100% in his devotion to Laurie.<br><br><i>Tate….</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=joe-manganiello-435-2.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379770052i/284596.jpg" alt="joe-manganiello-435" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh yes...speaking of the characters...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Tate's 10 year old son Jonas. A mostly sweet kid, but a bit too precocious for my tastes ( did not like him--a <b>10 year-old</b>- referring to Laurie as a "milf"! Should he even know what that means at 10? Maybe it's me, but I like 10 year-olds to act like they're 10, and not 16. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>But a minor annoyance and not enough to ruin the book for me.<br><br><i>Laurie and Tate...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=joe3-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379770052i/284595._SY540_.jpg" alt="joe3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To sum up, my third Kristen Ashley book was another winner and Tate and Laurie have to be my favorite characters so far. If you like a long, juicy story with plenty of heat and details, like badass heroes with a tender side, and love your heroines to get the HEA they deserve, then this is the book for you. So it was a little long...who cares? KA still kept me reading and hanging on her every word. 4 1/2 stars<br><br><i>*Thanks to Shawna for the perfect (for me) image of Tate...</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5671271959314327476" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer512159033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer779797146234373255"><br/><b>Amazon US ONLY: <a href='http://amzn.to/1LfEajx' rel='nofollow noopener'>'Sweet Dreams' by Kristen Ashley is ONLY .99 for a limited time</a></b> <-- click the link to purchase (check price before one-clicking).<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422407491i/13499371._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 4a959d91-22a3-41bf-8eb1-a8351a45d98b_zps7689a26a.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><u>December 31, 2013</u><br/><br/>Wanted to reread one of the old favorites [for the 4th time] to end the year on a high only a few authors can provide, KA being one of them. I might re-review this baby in a new year but everyone should really read this if only for one reason & that reason being: <br/><br/><b>Tatum Jackson</b> <br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388421254i/7831145._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo AdamCowieTateJacksonSweetDreams_zps0020efe7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><u>July, 2013</u><br/><br/><br/>Just read this again for the third (?) time I thin</span>
  <span id="freeText779797146234373255" style="display:none"><br><b>Amazon US ONLY: <a href="http://amzn.to/1LfEajx" rel="nofollow noopener">'Sweet Dreams' by Kristen Ashley is ONLY .99 for a limited time</a></b> &lt;-- click the link to purchase (check price before one-clicking).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422407491i/13499371._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4a959d91-22a3-41bf-8eb1-a8351a45d98b_zps7689a26a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><u>December 31, 2013</u><br><br>Wanted to reread one of the old favorites [for the 4th time] to end the year on a high only a few authors can provide, KA being one of them. I might re-review this baby in a new year but everyone should really read this if only for one reason &amp; that reason being: <br><br><b>Tatum Jackson</b> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388421254i/7831145._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo AdamCowieTateJacksonSweetDreams_zps0020efe7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>July, 2013</u><br><br><br>Just read this again for the third (?) time I think and it only gets better and better with each re-read! <br><br>While reading this, I realized that Kristen's characters remind me so much of John Hughes and his characters because none of them are perfect and they all have flaws most of us can relate to. I feel like I grew out of John's films (although, one can never really grow out of those, can they??) and graduated into Kristen's books in terms of age relatability (is that a word??).<br><br>Without sounding like a parrot, I want to say [again] that the main reason I adore Kristen's books is because she writes about people that are much closer to my age and happen to deal with the same shit I deal with daily (as in teengers with attitudes, etc.) yet she somehow manages to make real life exciting! So, as I read those, I keep thinking "maybe there is hope for me after all" ... LOL!<br><br><br>OK, back to the book ...<br><br>How effin sexy is Tate???? Hello!!! Talk about "Moist Factor 500" and I am not even talking about baked goods in this case ;) <br><br>So, to make it short and sweet:<br><br>Tate is the guy you want to be with;<br><br>Laurie is the chick you want to be (Tate would be the reason why + her family is "the shit" as Tate would put it);<br><br>Jonas is the kid you don't mind adopting;<br><br>Betty and Ned you don't mind adopting as your second set of parents;<br><br>Sunny and Shambles would make the grooviest budies because not only do they have the goods, they are also able to provide you with wicked baked goods when you get the munchies;<br><br>Krystal would be nice to have around if and when you need somebody to have your back (same with Twyla!);<br><br>Wood would make a great back up plan if things don't work out with Tate ... just sayin'<br><br><br>This was easy 5 stars for me! 1st, 2nd and 3rd time around :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="779797146234373255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
